Free Talk

Put a Smile on It 177

— Hai Ke

A—You were carousing at the brothel last night and didn’t get back until late into the night. Did your wife scold you?

B—No, no. The fact that I married a teacher is my great advantage. I was late coming home last night, and she was very civilized about it. She used the same method she used to punish elementary school students, making me write on the slate, “I must come home at 9 o’clock every night from now on,” a hundred times.

Patient (to a doctor who usually acts high and mighty) Doctor, I am pleasantly surprised that you have come so early today. Even my illness has improved somewhat.

Doctor—It's just that your western neighbor, Mr. Wang, suddenly took ill, and I was asked to come for a consultation, so I came to check on you. This is as the Western saying goes, “Kill two birds with one stone.”

Female A—I heard that you and your fiancé suddenly fell out. Is there any truth to this?

Female B—Yes, we fought very badly. We both made vows. I will no longer look at him, and he will no longer look at me. That day, I certainly didn’t look at him even once, but he was constantly sneaking glances at me.

Traveler (inspecting his room, to the innkeeper) This room is very stuffy, just like a prison. Innkeeper—Are you a prisoner, sir?

Tragic Death of Chinese Student at Purdue University in America 178

— Wang Jianhou

In mid-August, this newspaper's international telegraph carried a news item about the tragic death of Chinese student C. K. Shun in a car accident at Purdue University in the United States. Purdue University is located in West Lafayette, Indiana, in the United States, and is a well-known private university. Chen Shugui, a relative and a student at Shanghai Jiao Tong University, went to America last summer to study at that school. He and the aforementioned C. K. Shun, i.e., Sun Jiake, and Xu Baoquan, who died in the same car accident, were classmates and very good friends. The tragedy involving the two of them occurred while they were driving to Midesheng to welcome Chen. Although I did not kill Boren, Boren died because of me. Mr. Chen’s grief has reached its peak. He has entrusted me to tell readers about the beginning and end of the tragedy in the letter he sent to me.

Last year, there were more than 30 Chinese students at Purdue University, majoring in electrical engineering, mechanical engineering, and other subjects. After graduating this session, Mr. Chen went to an American factory in Midesheng for an internship during the summer vacation. As the internship was about to end, Mr. Xu and Mr. Sun wrote to Mr. Chen from West Lafayette, asking to drive their new car to Midesheng to welcome him back on a certain day. Mr. Chen waited for that day. Mr. Xu and Mr. Sun did drive from Lafayette toward Midesheng. Four Chinese classmates were sitting in the back seat of the car. They looked at the scenery along the way, sightseeing as they drove. They were in high spirits. However, Midesheng is an eleven-hour drive from Lafayette. Mr. Xu and his group left in the afternoon and estimated that they would not be able to reach their destination until midnight. Therefore, they stepped on the gas and drove quickly. They felt like they were flying, leaving the dust behind. Their speed had reached over sixty miles per hour. Unexpectedly, a car was driving towards them. Mr. Xu's car tried to avoid it, but it was too late to turn the engine off. Unexpectedly, the momentum was too fast, and the car suddenly lifted off the ground by a height of about ten feet. It overturned and rose up three times. The car was completely destroyed. Mr. Xu and Mr. Sun died tragically. When the car first overturned, the car’s awning was shattered by the impact. The four people sitting in the car were all thrown out, escaping with their lives. They were lucky.

Mr. Xu was from Minhou. He was previously a student at William Penn University in America. Mr. Sun was from Tianjin. He was previously a student at Nankai University in our country. The two men were only just over twenty years old. They were good at sports, proficient in music, skilled at photography, driving, and swimming. It is most regrettable that both men’s families were rich, and they themselves had exceptional talents. They studied diligently in their courses and their grades were outstanding. As a result, the teachers and students in the entire school praised them. Among the hundreds of graduates this session, forty-two students were awarded honors degrees. Only three of the Chinese students won this honor. Namely, Mr. Chen Shugui and the two deceased men. The three men were the same age, had the same ambitions, and went out together. They had only been classmates for a year, but they were as close as brothers. In their spare time after class, they often worked together to plan major projects for industrial salvation. They looked forward to returning home after completing their studies, building their motherland, and bringing happiness to society. Who would have thought that a sudden misfortune would strike and they would die tragically in a foreign country? It is heartbreaking. First, Mr. Sun's sister also had a car in America. When she left America to go to Europe this summer, her younger brother wanted it. His sister refused to give it to him, saying, “My brother likes to take risks, I’m afraid it will cause trouble.” How would she know that he would die because of it? Mr. Xu had been away from the country for a long time, and his 73-year-old father was looking forward to his beloved son’s return day and night. When the bad news came, he shed tears of grief and was heartbroken.

That day, Mr. Chen received the news and rushed back from Midesheng, weeping with grief. He helped Mr. Ke Zhongzheng, a ten-year friend of Mr. Xu, to take care of the funeral arrangements. On September 5, he held a funeral for the two men in Lafayette. On that day, Chinese and foreign relatives and friends, as well as teachers and students from Purdue, all came to pay their respects. The professors also wrote articles in the newspaper to mourn them, imagining that the two men's learning and morals were valued by their peers.

Mr. Ke and Mr. Xu’s sister escorted the remains of the two men back to China on the Queen of Asia on the 3rd of this month. They had previously entrusted my elder brother to arrange all the transfer matters, so that the bones could be buried in their homeland as soon as possible. If their souls are aware, may they return soon. I can’t help but feel a sense of sorrow when I touch this three-foot bronze coffin. Therefore, I wrote this account.

Records of Fan Mating 179

— Zheng Yimei

Miss Qian Yunshan, the daughter of the renowned painter, Cloud Crane, possessed a deep-seated family artistic background. She excelled in painting and composing poetry. She once created a fan painted with flowers in the style of Nantian, exuding pure fragrance and elegance, untouched by contemporary trends. This fan eventually came to the attention of Li Youzhu. Youzhu, a distinguished gentleman from Luhe, deeply loved painting and calligraphy. After appreciating the fan, he was reluctant to part with it. Learning that Yunshan was still unmarried, he entrusted a friend to act as a matchmaker and propose marriage. The auspicious event was successfully arranged, and on the Double Tenth Festival this year, they celebrated the joy of their union. The new bride, carefully applying makeup, diligently prepared decorations before the wedding, creating four painted screens and a hanging scroll to adorn the bridal chamber. Each painting was accompanied by a poem, all fresh and delightful. For example, on the plum blossom, bamboo, and longevity belt painting, it was written: "Red plum blossoms and green bamboo fill the garden with spring; again, the Zhaohua blooms, witnessing the new year. Glad that the painting enhances longevity, bring it to wish health to the elders." On the lotus pond and kingfisher painting: "Ten miles of lotus pond after the rain; a dragonfly stays on a leaf. A kingfisher flies past, bringing poetic imagery; a painted boat carries wine for an evening cool stroll." On the autumn sunflowers and yellow bird painting: "Autumn sunflowers and dahlias compete in fragrance; brought from overseas, they are unusually beautiful. The small bird flies high, seemingly mistaking them for peonies, the Wei Purple and Yao Yellow." On the camellia and pair of sparrows painting: "Secluded in a small pavilion with heavy curtains, I only love to chant and drink. I remember the snow melting on the flower path, a pair of frozen sparrows chirping on the sunny eaves." The hanging scroll was inscribed with a five-character律 poem: "Painting learned from famous masters; prosperity appears before my eyes. The brocade hall is newly rich and noble; the Yao Island is a small paradise. Fortunately, the flowers are always beautiful; happily, we meet when the moon is full. Hanging high on the powder wall, may it wish for longevity." The auspicious language is particularly appropriate. Her calligraphy is also elegant and free. Such talent in a woman is rare. One can imagine the joy in the bridal chamber, no less than Zhao Songxue and Lady Guan, playfully working with clay, without distinction between "you" and "I." Such a beautiful and harmonious marriage adds another brilliant page to the history of tenderness.

Gleanings from Autumn Sounds 180

— Shuangqiu

Nengren Temple is one of the Eight Heroic Daughters and Sons stories. Yiqiu plays Zhang Jinfeng. With light makeup and simple clothing, she perfectly embodies the charm of a young lady from a modest family. Both with heavy and light makeup, Yiqiu is beautiful, but this play is the most suitable for appreciating her natural beauty. She has many singing parts and her melodies are beautiful. When Thirteenth Sister proposes marriage, her expression is shy, pretending to laugh, and enchantingly beautiful. Paired with Furongcao's Thirteenth Sister, whose demeanor is poised and whose words are candid, they complement each other perfectly.

Mandarin Duck Tomb is a tragic play of the noblest, purest, and deepest love. Due to the lack of freedom in marriage and the constraints of old morality, yet without the courage to break free from the family, both sides devote themselves to love without return, and ultimately decide to sacrifice their lives for it. They are the most pitiful of infatuated lovers. Yiqiu plays Wang Wujie, with *Siping Diao*, seven-character *Erhuang*, and *Fan Erhuang*. The complexity and effort of her singing, and the novelty and mellowness of her melodies, surpass all other singing. Her tragic expression and sorrowful tone can cause viewers and listeners to grieve and shed tears uncontrollably. One can say her skills are divine. Having gained fame in Beijing and Shanghai, her performances are widely praised. This time, paired with Jiang Miaoxiang's Xie Zhaolang and Furongcao's Wang Sao, it is the perfect addition to perfection, truly a masterpiece of sorrow and beauty.

A Record of a Day Trip 181

— Yu Jianhua

In the autumn of the year of Gengwu, I was about to open a personal painting exhibition in Shanghai. I spent my days painting and never put down my brush, which exhausted my spirit. Therefore, on the afternoon of the Mid-Autumn Festival, I went on a trip with more than ten female alumni from the Patriotic Girls' School. When we arrived at Paotaiwan, I went to Baoshan alone with four or five people. Baoshan borders the river and the sea, and is located at the intersection of the Yangtze and Huangpu Rivers. It is also close to Shanghai, so it should be a major town. However, the city is small and sparsely populated, seemingly unable to bear its desolation. We entered through the South Gate and got off the bus at the Drum Tower, which is the center of the city. To the west, we visited the elementary school, where the trees cast shadows and there was a beautiful terrace pond. To the south was the Public Education Center, which was converted from the City God Temple. Last year, the City God was said to have lost his head, which was widely rumored. Now, it has been completely swept away, while the City God in Shanghai remains majestic amidst the incense smoke, receiving the worship of the world. So, even gods can be fortunate or unfortunate. We visited the Normal School, which bordered the city wall. On top of the majestic battlements, there was a tower called Wangjiang (Looking at the River). The misty waves stretched as far as the eye could see, with three or five sailboats rising and falling in between. A line stretched across the horizon, which was Chongming Island. We exited through the West Gate and went to the park. The park was quite small. We followed the river embankment, where the deep grass reached our shins. The wooden stakes along the embankment resembled long combs. We entered through the North Gate and took a carriage back to Paotaiwan. We ate on a large rock on the abandoned embankment. A gentle breeze blew and the river water surged, leaping with a "xiong" sound. My fellow traveler, Chen Sheng, was startled and fled, but I stopped him and he stood there timidly. Everyone watching laughed joyously. As dusk fell, we walked to Wusong and took a bus back to school. After dinner, as the fun of the trip had not yet subsided, I gathered dozens of students and went out to admire the moon. We left the school and walked along Jiangwan Road, laughing and talking, running and galloping, until we returned from North Sichuan Road. At that time, the moon was as bright as a mirror, and the night was as cool as water, with wisps of clouds reluctant to leave the moonlight. The shadows of the trees swayed along the road, and we could occasionally hear the sounds of finger-guessing games from people's homes. When I returned to school, it was already late. I took out my unfinished painting and added some finishing touches. The moonlight shone in through the cracks in the window, as if comforting my loneliness.

Impressions of Belgium (Part 2) 182

— Wang Yachen

Continuing to look closer, I realized that all were oil painted scenes. The upper part of the scenery directly reaches the skylight of the circular building, taking light to match the outdoors. A mud ditch is built below, arranging the scenes of the Waterloo area of that year. Lying horizontally in the soil were all wounded soldiers and dead horses, with blurred blood and flesh...too gruesome to look at. Each part of the painting has an explanation. This picture was made by the Belgian academic painter Di Sansi, using realistic brushwork and impressionistic colors. It is praised as a great picture, and the painting style is also novel. It cannot be compared with ordinary scene paintings. After finishing the visit, we went forward to see the monuments erected by various countries. After walking about five miles, we saw another monument. Beside the monument were carved drooping..., also objects commemorating Napoleon. Today's Waterloo, fields connected by ridges, is wide and open for dozens of miles. Only a few monuments remain. Only the place name is known to the world. All foreigners who come to Belgium are eager to visit. I visited there for four hours, only arousing a sense of history.

The city hall of the three capitals of Belgium. The city halls of most European countries are famous buildings in history. The city hall of Beijing, Belgium, was built in Gothic style (the style of ancient Rome). The solemn grandeur and the exquisite details of its carvings can be compared with the Notre Dame Cathedral in Paris. Opposite is the old White Palace, with a square in the middle. There are dozens of flower stalls in the square. The famous flowers are blooming, set off by the lofty and elegant architecture, which is particularly spectacular. Entering the city hall through the square, you need to buy a ticket to visit. Entering the interior, no matter where you look, it is beautiful. Dozens of portraits of celebrities are displayed on the walls, all painted by Dutch painters. To the right, there is another hall. Sixteen woven portraits are hung on the four walls. The weaving is extremely exquisite, and the combination of light and color is appropriate. Looking at it from a distance, it is like a famous painting. It is almost impossible to distinguish it as a woven object. From here, enter the council hall. Antique tables and chairs are placed in the middle. The four walls are inlaid with famous paintings. The remaining utensils are also extremely delicate. From the council hall to the right, enter several offices in the city hall. There are also famous paintings on the walls. Finally, visit a chapel, which is set up for the people in the hall to offer new prayers. In the center of the hall, there is an image of Jesus, and several candlestick holders are placed below, like the temples in our country. The light in the hall is not bright, and the furnishings are neat, which makes people feel solemn. After leaving the city hall, take a tram to the suburbs near Beijing, Belgium. The place name is Lagu. There is a park there. The garden is only a little more than ten acres, with exotic flowers competing to bloom and green trees covering the sky. Behind the park is a forest, separated by a lake, which does not allow visitors to pass. Artificial beauty and natural beauty are far away from each other. It is truly a great place for tourists to rest. Then, walk along the avenue to the right outside the park for twenty minutes and arrive at another park. This park has a Chinese pagoda, which is dozens of feet high, and several Japanese-style pavilions. It is said that this was transported from the Panama Fair in the past. There is also an Oriental Art Museum, which displays Chinese and Japanese antiques. The visit was hurried, and I did not remember it. The Lagu area has royal residences. The road is extremely clean, and the trees planted along the road are neat. There are also woods for pedestrians to pass through. In the shadows of the setting sun, it is especially lovely. I lingered in the deep forest and forgot to return until dusk before returning to the hostel.

European Travel Correspondence (Seventy-Eight) 183

— Liu Haisu

Diary of a Tour of Italy

(3) Ten Days in Rome (1)

— The Immortal City — La Vile eternelle —

June 1st — Exhibition of Spanish Masterpieces and Exhibition of Modern Japanese Paintings

We arrived in Rome early in the morning of June 1st. When we finished the 36-hour long journey and walked into this immortal ancient city, we all felt very happy. Especially I, who had a passionate admiration for the things in Rome, felt very proud.

Leaving the station, we were led by a guide who spoke broken French to a hotel not far from the station to stay. He said that this was a hotel where French people used to live. It cost twelve lire per person per day. The rooms were also tall and elegant. Everyone was very satisfied. This road is called Via Principe Vmberto, which is a ten-minute walk from the train station. It is very convenient to go anywhere. This is considered a suitable location in Rome.

Rome, which I had been looking forward to for many years, was finally realized. We were all eager to walk into that beautiful, grand, and mysterious treasure house. So, after washing up at the hotel, we hurried out. When walking on the streets of Rome, it was like being completely separated from the modern world. Everywhere we saw ruins and stone pillars. Those ancient Roman cultural relics, exposed to the wind and rain for a long two to three thousand years, were transmitted to our eyes. We couldn't help but see ourselves as a small, short, and impermanent illusion, just passing by in front of it. Not only the ancient relics, but also the houses, shops, and walls along the way were all dark tea-yellow. Under the bright sunlight, they showed a desolate and ancient atmosphere. However, in all this ancient appearance, the windows and doors of all the houses were painted with jade-like eye-piercing bright green. Just like walking in the alleys of Beijing and seeing the big red doors everywhere, there was a similar sting.

Walking to the center of the stone-paved square in front of the station, we took the No. MP public motorcycle to the New Art Museum to see the Spanish masterpiece exhibition. This was what we had inquired and learned about when we were leisurely planning today's itinerary on the road. We knew that today was Italy's Unification Day, and all museums and art galleries were closed. Therefore, we planned to see the Spanish famous painting exhibition in the morning and the Japanese modern art exhibition in the afternoon. Today, the Italians are enthusiastically celebrating their National Founding Day. The Italian flag with red, white, and green colors is flying all over the streets. The naive and optimistic citizens who permeate the entire city of Rome are singing their national anthem. A burst of applause and a burst of shouts, joy poured out from their hearts like flowing water. I have rarely seen such an atmosphere. The motorcycle twisted and turned up and down. The stone pillars, fountains, and sculptures in the squares everywhere were always surprising.

Gold Market in a Hesitant State 184

Market conditions contain a lazy component

Silver prices may rebound

A glance at the gold market situation yesterday, the 13th, showed a hesitant trend, with ups and downs. Yarn and Flower Market Boosted by Foreign Yarn and Flowers 188

The yarn market is slightly firm, but the overall situation remains calm. The price of American cotton’s Three Grades of yarn has risen, leading some people to become bullish. However, the current yarn sales have not seen a significant increase, and the price of 20-count Blue Phoenix yarn has recently fallen sharply due to accumulated inventory. The previous purchases by Sichuan and Gaoyang groups are now being sold off, making the current yarn market extremely weak. There is a risk of further price declines in the future, as prices are too high and business could stop at any moment. However, forward contracts are relatively tight due to a lack of sellers, although most people are bearish. It is said that one manufacturer's attitude remains firm and unchanged.

In recent months, the "Ren Biao" market has rebounded slightly. At the opening of the "Ren Biao" market, due to the continuous rise of American cotton, there were not many sellers in the market, and the atmosphere was relatively tight. Prices rose by three, four, five, and nine "qian" respectively. In the afternoon, it was reported that the price of Three Grades of yarn had risen slightly, with prices rising by two, three, and five "qian" for each month. The total transaction volume for the day was 11,950 bales. It was found that Dafeng sold 700 bales, Daji 400 bales, Taichang 400 bales, Shenchang 400 bales, Yiyu 450 bales, and the rest 200 bales. Yuande bought 800 bales, Yichang 550 bales, Yuda 400 bales, and Yijun 450 bales. The closing prices of "Ren Biao" are recorded on the left:

Current yarn sales are 1,200 bales. Current yarn sales are still good. It was found that the total purchase volume of various groups throughout the day was 1,200 bales. Among the customer groups, the mainland took in 250 bales, Guangdong 300 bales, Luzhou 60 bales, Changsha 75 bales, Sichuan 40 bales, Shantou 120 bales, Yunnan 90 bales, Hankou 55 bales, and miscellaneous groups 140 bales.

Cotton Market Shows Signs of Rebound 189

The cotton market is trending upward, with a sudden rebound. This is because the American cotton situation has stabilized, and the declining trend has subsided. Therefore, Japanese merchants are taking the opportunity to buy up large quantities, about 20,000 "dan" in two days. With such a large volume of purchases, the market has been emptied, and the atmosphere is relatively tight. In addition, some people believe that the American cotton rescue organization and the Japanese merchants' buying spree are temporarily a positive sign, with prices possibly reaching 32 "liang" for each month. However, current cotton transactions are still light. Future steps will still depend on the American flower situation and actual sales.

The "Han Biao" market rebounded by four "qian." At the opening of the "Han Biao" market, due to the continuous rise of American cotton, there were few sellers in the market, and the atmosphere was relatively tight. Prices rose by 0.25 "qian" for each month. In the afternoon, Japanese merchants and some others bought up large quantities, and the market atmosphere became even stronger, with prices rising by 0.15 to 0.2 "qian" respectively. The total transaction volume for the day was 61,900 "dan." It was found that Lichang bought 6,400 "dan," Gongtai 3,200 "dan," Yuchang 3,400 "dan," Shenyu 2,800 "dan," Yuande 2,900 "dan," Daji 2,600 "dan," and the rest from 1,000 to 1,300 "dan." Jinfeng sold 3,400 "dan," Shenchang 1,000 "dan," Daji 2,600 "dan," and the rest from various firms. The closing prices of "Han Biao" are recorded on the left:

Indian Cotton Purchases by Japanese Merchants Remain Strong 191

Due to political reasons, the Bombay market was closed for three days last week, with little business. Prices followed the weakness of American cotton, but brokers and exporters bought when prices fell, which hindered the downward trend. Export demand remains good, with transactions in Oomra and Pingul cotton. There have also been inquiries from Europe. It is reported that as of October 3rd, Japan has purchased 800 bales of new cotton and 7,500 bales of old cotton. The statistics for the past week are appended below (in thousands of bales):

The spot market in Liverpool was quiet last week. Futures were not affected by the US government's cotton report, which was not beyond general expectations. Short selling was slight, but buying on dips was also not weak. The market situation throughout the week was unremarkable. Egyptian cotton prices fell slightly due to a cotton harvest report favorable to sellers.

Grain and Rice Market Remains Weak 192

In Zhabei, over a hundred boats arrived over the past few days, causing congestion due to abundant supply, and prices fell accordingly. New japonica rice has been gradually declining since the Double Tenth Festival, with a total drop of one yuan. Yesterday, it weakened by another 0.20 to 0.30 yuan. Top-grade rice has already entered the inner city at 17 yuan, opening at around 16.80 yuan.

The general trend for average grades stabilized during the evening session due to slightly improved demand. New indica rice turned flat yesterday, with no price movement. However, in the previous two sessions, it fell by 0.80 to 0.90 yuan following the trend of western japonica rice. Currently, special top-grade rice opens at 14.60 to 14.70 yuan, with a mediocre market situation. The supply of "Du Jian" rice is not abundant, and existing inventory has not been selling well, leaving room for further price adjustments. Special high-grade rice barely opens at 13 yuan. The market for "Yang Xian" rice has settled after the price decline. Inquiries are still strong in this street, with prices opening at 12.40 to 12.50 yuan. It is found that this year's harvest in Zhejiang province is very abundant. There is no prospect of strong sales of this "Yang Du Jian" rice in Zhejiang province, so it would not be surprising if it continues to soften in the future. Special customer-grade rice opens at 11 yuan, while medium-grade rice is only around 9.50 yuan. The overall situation is still weak, with a decline of about 0.20 yuan yesterday. Shipments of "Bu Jian" rice are slightly scarce, and small lots are still being sold. The high price is 11.50 yuan, with a weary outlook. "Bai Yuan" rice is stagnant, with sluggish sales, and has declined by as much as one yuan since the festival. Currently, the high price is 16.30 to 16.40 yuan. New "Yin Yuan" rice only has sporadic supply, which is maintaining demand, so the market has remained stable throughout. Top-grade rice is at 15.60 yuan.

In Shanghai South, over thirty boats arrived yesterday. Sales in this street are extremely weak. "Chang Bang" new rice continued to fall by 0.30 yuan, opening at 16.30 to 16.40 yuan. "Su Tong Bang" rice is also softening, with high-grade rice returning to the 15 yuan range. Transactions are few, and the market trend is poor. "Nan Bang Qing Jiao" and other kiln varieties of indica rice are arriving in increasing quantities, with sluggish sales. Merchants are eager to sell off their inventory, so prices have been continuously cut. Yesterday, it fell by another 0.30 to 0.40 yuan. The general price here is 13.50 to 13.60 yuan. As for "Ting Lin" and other white rice, although demand is weak, prices have only softened slightly due to low supply. "Yang Jian" rice mostly opens at 10.08 to 10.09 yuan, while high-grade "Du Jian" rice is at 12.00 yuan, with a drop of 0.20 to 0.30 yuan. The overall trend is extremely weak. High-grade rice from factory machines is priced at around 10 yuan. There is some demand from rural areas, and the market is also softening.

Distant Futures for Flour Enter the 3 Qian Range 193

Yesterday, the flour market saw a consistent and sharp decline in all months. The recent months were particularly hard hit by factory sell-offs. Distant future contracts, particularly those for January and February, saw a gradual decline, falling to as low as 2 taels 2 qian 9.5 fen, entering the 2 taels 3 qian range. Contracts for December to February all approached the 2 taels 3 qian level. This was due to renewed reports of falling prices for imported foreign wheat, and the market sentiment was already bearish. In addition to foreign wheat already arrived at port, factories were expecting two more shipments to arrive soon, prompting widespread sell-offs. Customer demand stalled, and the market consensus was for further declines, leading to a general weakness. At the close, the contracts for October and November each fell by 3 fen, December by 2 fen, January by 2.25 fen, February by 1.75 fen, and March by 2.5 fen.

Recent Wheat Prices Plummet by 5-6 Fen 194

The wheat market yesterday opened with a weak price. Continuing reports of arriving foreign wheat and further discounts on foreign wheat prompted Shanghai merchants to continue to place orders at attractive prices. Some factories immediately hedged by selling futures, further depressing the market. In the afternoon, market sentiment turned even more bearish, and prices continued to fall. At the close, October contracts were down by 6 fen, November by 5 fen, December by 3 fen, January by 2 fen, February by 3 fen, and March by 4 fen. While the supply of domestic bran and wheat is limited, existing stockpiles are sufficient. The arrival of more foreign wheat is further dampening the market. Yesterday, Fufeng Factory purchased nearly 10,000 packages of wheat from Niuzhuang, Yaowan, Shashi, and Jiangbei, causing prices to fall by another 1 qian.

Silk and Tea Processing in Shanghai Still Struggling to Improve 195

Yesterday's raw silk market in Shanghai continued to show some firmness. European firms are reportedly buying Shanghai white raw silk futures, but factory silk costs are still high, and they are unwilling to sell at a loss. Furthermore, raw material supplies are dwindling, making transactions increasingly difficult. Yesterday, only Dachang and others halted trades for 30 packages of Shanghai white raw silk futures. Kechang purchased 8 packages of yellow coarse silk, and prices remained firm.

High-Grade Zhenmei Tea from Gaozhuang Sees Slight Movement in Sales to France 196

Yesterday, the sales of high-grade Zhenmei green tea from Gaozhuang, Wuyuan, to French firms showed slight improvement. Top-quality "Chouxin" tea opened at 200 taels, unchanged from last week. However, tea from Tunxi and Suian areas fell by another 2-3 taels. Jinlong Foreign Firm also slightly increased its purchases of "Fengmei" and "Zhucha" teas from larger wholesalers, but prices were extremely low. Tongfu has already begun processing Qimen black tea, and the Russian Aid Association began sampling tea yesterday, suggesting a potential for business. However, tea market prices are currently at extremely low levels. The overall trend has already reached its limits.

Melton Cloth, Used for Western Suits and Uniforms, is Scarce and Pricey 197

Melton cloth, specifically used for Western suits and uniform tops, comes in both plain and patterned varieties, with varying quality. Lower-grade cloths sell for only 1.1-1.2 taels per yard, while higher-grade cloths, such as those from Deke and Dulanxiang, can sell for 2.25 taels. Current market sales are exceptionally strong, and the Cloth Guild's sales prices have also increased sharply. Large transactions are currently difficult to secure, as existing inventories are low, and sellers are raising prices in anticipation of higher profits. Compared to last year, prices have increased by over 3 qian per yard. Those seeking "Changqing" fabric must also add a few fen. Plain-colored cloths are also extremely firm. Yesterday, Hwa Kee, Hwa Po, and An Lee brands were sold at 1.9 taels net, while Taihe's top-grade "Flower" brand was at 2.05 taels, and the second-grade was at 1.55 taels.

Mixed Fortunes for Domestic and Foreign Piece Goods 198

There have been no significant changes for locally produced fabrics recently. However, Hubei "Tian Zi Zu" cloth is in short supply, selling for 8.35 taels yesterday. Coarse twill from Tianjin and Henan is seeing increased activity. "Mao Ying" suddenly faces demand exceeding supply, opening at 5.05 taels. Fine cloth remains sluggish, with "Lan Shuang Yu" opening at 6.85 taels, "Yang He Cai Qiu" at 6.825 taels, and "Lan Ji" at 6.65 taels, with extremely poor sales. Bleached cloth has recently become slightly more active, with merchants from this street and Ningbo and Tianjin purchasing. "Jin San Ta" is selling for 7.4 taels, and "Yun Wai Piao Xiang" for 7.6 taels, though velvet is slightly soft.

Eastern and Western piece goods softened yesterday. The previous sharp increase in prices led to sluggish actual sales, causing market sentiment to suddenly become bearish. Yesterday, "Zhi Gong Ni" fell by 2.5 li, with "Mo Qian Shan" opening at 3 qian 1 fen 7 li 5 hao, "La Yan" at 3 qian 2 fen 2 li 5 hao, and "Shuang Tong Lu" at 2 qian 9 fen. Fine broadcloth remains firm, with "Hu Xin Ting" still opening at 2 qian 9 fen 5 hao, and "Zi Jin Shan" at 2 qian 9 fen 2 li 5 hao. However, "Tu Lan Hui" fell by 7.5 li to 1 fen due to abundant supply. "Zhi Gong Duan" saw a sharp decline, with lower-quality goods falling by 2.5 li to 5 li, while higher-quality goods remained unchanged. Among all goods, only the "Four Gentlemen" "Zhi Gong Ni" from both domestic and foreign factories stands out, opening at 2 qian 8 fen yesterday. Western goods remain sluggish.

Southern and Northern Goods: Black Dates and Walnuts Available 199

Since the new crop of black dates became available, the volume of recent arrivals has increased sharply. It is estimated that the Shandong cargo ship delivered thousands of packages that have yet to be released. Yesterday, southern market businesses released over seventy packages of previous crop dates, priced at eleven taels, a slight easing compared to before. Yesterday, more than one hundred packages of new Jinan walnuts were sold for ten taels and two qian. The market was still active and the trend remained flat.

Metals and Bamboo Products: "Jie Gang" Steel Continues to Fall 200

Since the arrival of "Zhu Jie Gang" steel resulted in sluggish inventory, prices have been declining. Recently, the downward trend has not stopped, with prices continuing to fall. The current market price for standard patterns is 85 taels, and even better-quality patterns are only valued at 90 taels. It is reported that construction companies such as Xin Jin Ji and Feng Tai Xing have been receiving shipments in recent days, resulting in limited demand. The market is reporting daily sales of only 70 to 80 tons.

Central Grand Theater announces: "One Thousand and One Nights" is a famous Arabian tale that is popular among people in the East and West. It can be considered one of the most interesting pages in "One Thousand and One Nights". It has been adapted into a film by Ye Yisheng, a member of the art community and film director. The entire film has now been completed. The photography, set design, scene arrangement, and costumes all have unexpected contributions. Once test-screened, it was amazing. However, Buping overhears this and comes to her rescue alone. The henchmen are terrified at the sight of him because they have all been defeated by him in the past. Under Zhou Long's command, they have no choice but to surround and attack him. However, Buping's martial arts are superb. He darts and jumps, as agile as a swallow. Although there are dozens of henchmen, none can get close to him. Zhou Long is extremely anxious and orders Huang Yong to help. However, Huang Yong is soon knocked down by Buping. In the end, Buping accidentally triggers a mechanism and is captured. This scene is tightly paced, the mechanism is ingenious, and the performances are realistic. It is a rare masterpiece among domestic films.

Youth Corner

Impressions of a Northern Journey 221

— Su Ling

(13) Drunken Night

Every day, I am woken up very early by my classmates to go sketching in the countryside.

At night, everyone is idle. After several hours of chatting, we go to bed. This time, Mr. Feng and Mr. Liao invited me out for a bite to eat or a drink.

We left the inn and walked through some dark streets, looking for a relatively clean restaurant.

"Outside the North Gate, when I came back from sketching during the day, I saw a Tianjin-style restaurant. It's good and cheap," Liao said.

"What's it called?"

"I forgot the name, but we'll know when we get there. It's opposite a tall building, yes, opposite a photo studio."

"Is it far? It's already nine o'clock," I said.

"It doesn't matter, what does it matter?"

So we went looking.

It was a small Tianjin canteen. We went in and took a table.

Twenty minutes later, we were drinking.

"How is this northern cuisine, Mr. Xu, can you get used to it?"

"Oh, it's very good, very good," I said, picking up a piece of spicy chicken. "This, I think this is very delicious, but that fish is not bad either."

"Drink, drink."

So everyone drank a few glasses. The waiter brought a second pot, then a third pot of wine.

"Let's get drunk tonight, we won't stop until we're drunk."

"Why? Getting drunk is annoying."

I used to be able to drink a bit, but after getting very drunk once during the Lunar New Year, I didn't want to drink anymore. In recent years, although I often went to a small restaurant with a few friends for a glass or two, I never dared to drink too much. Tonight's amount of alcohol is probably the most I've had in years. I was very afraid of getting dizzy, and tried hard to stay calm, but Feng was already a bit excitedly confused.

"Let's not drink anymore, it's getting late. Isn't there a curfew after twelve o'clock?"

So we left the restaurant, and stumbled drunkenly through the dark alleys, only Liao was relatively sober, because he drank less. Feng was really drunk, staggering, talking excitedly, his drunken breath wafting in the night air.

Autumn Wind 222

— Photographed by Nan Sun

"Haha, Mr. Xu, I, I tell you, my" woman is from your hometown, she loves me, but she doesn't understand me at all, she doesn't understand my art..."

"People are all the same, I have been deceived by people...I had a glorious past, now I am silent, no, my heart has not been cold because of silence...Why do I engage in art...But my woman doesn't understand me..."

Groping along the dark street, we stumbled back to the inn, Feng not stopping his talking.

(14) Mountain Climbing

I haven't climbed a mountain in two or three years. Although I am not old, my behavior seems to have aged. But this time, climbing a mountain with this group of young people (actually, I am also young), I felt very excited.

Before climbing the mountain, everyone bought a wooden staff.

This is a mountain with no people and no temples. Although it is not very high, it is steep, so going up is not very easy.

So everyone started to climb.

I hadn't reached a third of the way, and I was already very weak, clinging to branches, climbing with almost both hands as feet, panting, my heart pounding violently, and resting on the ground. But there were still people behind me. Fat Feng and Miss Zi in her high heels were really exhausted.

So I remembered the courage and strength I had two years ago in Nanjing, walking from Xuanwu Lake to Zijin Mountain, climbing to the highest peak, and then walking back to the city gate. I really felt that I am old now, my youth has passed.

No, I must continue to climb up. I want to restore my youthful enthusiasm and courage. I want to climb up, I want to boast to the young people, although I am your teacher—a teacher who has broken his innocence—but my spirit and body are still as lively, passionate, and brave as yours...

Finally, everyone reached the summit.

The wind blew our sweat-soaked clothes, soothing the brave but exhausted energy of this group of children. The forest was howling, and the blurred scenery unfolded before our eyes.

We all lay down to rest, looking up at the sky, the sun shining on us.

Yang was the first to climb up, waving a small flag. Song never seemed to know fatigue. He brought his painting gear, a thermos of hot water, and food to satisfy his hunger. When he reached the summit, he set up his easel and started painting. But I really admired Miss Yu's courage in climbing to the top of the mountain in high heels.

After the fatigue of resting subsided slightly, the sun was gradually setting in the west. We all tidied up our clothes and prepared to descend the mountain, but Song's painting was not yet finished.

"Mr. Xu, don't rush, come and revise the painting. Let those who walk slowly go first."

So I quickly revised it for him. He packed up his things, a large pile on his back, and ran down a steep, straight mountain path. When the people who left first were still at the foot of the mountain, he was already shouting down below.

Going down the mountain was easier than going up, but the fatigue was probably even greater than going up, and our mouths were excessively parched. So we asked a village family for cool water to drink.

The village women were very shy and curious, peeking at us. Several large dogs barked wildly.

In Front of a Tree 223

— Photographed by Nan Sun

Vanguard Weekly, Issue 16 224

The Vanguard Weekly, published by the Vanguard Society, has been highly praised by people from all walks of life since its publication, and is a revival publication in the Chinese literary world. Moreover, the colleagues of the society work very hard, and the 16th issue has now been published. The content includes "The Subject Matter of Nationalist Literature and Art", "The People", "Freedom and Cracking Scalps", "Two Orphans" and other works, which are all texts that modern young people must read. Each copy sells for three copper coins, and major bookstores in Shanghai and the gatehouses of various schools are available for sale.

Fudan Re-Joins Jiangda Movement 225

Less than two weeks after the start of this semester, I heard students talking about Fudan re-joining the Jiangda Movement. The arrival of this good news really surprised and delighted me. Wasn't Fudan a member of the Jiangda Association before? Due to some small matters, they developed the intention to withdraw. Now they are willing to re-join. There is nothing between the two sides. It shows that everyone can understand and eliminate previous private opinions, and focus on the international position. I can't help but feel fortunate for the future of Chinese sports. Of course, it is not because Fudan joins that the future of Chinese sports can be celebrated, it is because everyone can be self-aware and willing to work together.

Now let me talk about the recent sports situation at Fudan.

Here I must first make a statement. Fudan was not unconcerned with sports before. Due to the withdrawal from the Jiangda Games, there were fewer places to participate and perform, and heroes had no place to use their talents. Interest in various sports was relatively diluted.

After this re-joining, less than two weeks after the start of school, notices about sports on campus were visible everywhere. The school and private organizations were recruiting soldiers and selecting players, holding meetings... in a variety of ways, making a lot of noise. Some of them even set up women's sections.

Recently, in order to popularize student sports, the school held a championship competition for various colleges, which is currently underway. Private organizations are also challenging each other.

There is no need for me to say more about the reputation of cross-country running in Shanghai. Everyone knows it. Every evening and morning, on Xiangyin Road and by the racetrack, you can see a group of brave and vigorous athletes competing and running to create their records.

It goes without saying that on campus, during extracurricular time, clusters of male and female students are practicing their ball skills on the sports field. It seems that one must have a strong physique to study. (Qing)

Art World

Picasso on Art Books 226

— Translated by Chen Deming

Picasso, a strange talent in the modern French art world, is a great painter of the Post-Impressionist school, the leader of Cubism, and the founder of Fauvism. He is truly a versatile person. It is most appropriate to call him the Don Juan (a versatile and handsome man praised in the poems of Byron, the great poet) in the art world. However, because his art is infinitely changeable, his attitude is extremely elusive. A mysterious mist often surrounds him, making it difficult for people to see his true face. The main reason is that he usually only paints and does not speak. Recently, he suddenly became interested and wrote a long book on art, which was reprinted in the famous French art magazine Formes. In this letter, he fully revealed his artistic views, and made every effort to ridicule and scold the current general hypocrisy in art. The importance and value of this letter goes without saying. Therefore, I urgently translated it to share with readers. (The following is Picasso's letter) Translator's note.

People usually think of me as an explorer.

I don't explore, I just discover occasionally.

Some people have turned Cubism into a physical exercise. We see weak people pretending to be physically strong every day. They think that by turning things into squares, they can obtain the effect of "strength". My most logical works, made with all my strength, are taken by them to produce mechanical things devoid of reality.

For example, you see "a famous Cubist painter", he is a person who "achieved his goal".

Around 1900, his father said to him, "My son, I will send you to Paris to learn new art." He obeyed. As soon as he arrived in Paris, he began to produce new art works. These new art works are comparable to the art works in "Spring Magazine" (referring to low-level French art, which Picasso cites to ridicule the new art writer).

You can imagine how much it pains me to see people imitating my art, my works, and even my methods.

One day, several clever Surrealist writers saw several sketches and pencil drawings in my sketchbook with only a few dots and lines. The facts are as follows - I greatly admired astronomical charts. I discovered a sense of beauty in them beyond their scientific representation. Therefore, one day I started to draw a picture with many dots connected by lines, and some dots not connected by lines, representing the stars in the sky. My intention was to use this composition in a realistic work in the future as part of it. But these Surrealists, oh, they are really smart, they all said in a firm tone that these compositions fit their abstract ideas.

I remember an event that happened in 1925, when several friends insisted on inviting me to visit that absurd exhibition representing low-level taste, although it had some educational value - the International Exhibition of Decorative Arts. They said to me, "Picasso, you will see that all the products there are influenced by you. You will find yourself in it. You will recognize that those works are your handiwork." They said this probably to please me.

Imagine Michael Angelo being invited to a banquet by several friends, and those friends standing up to welcome him and saying, "We have just had someone send over -

Page 24

a Renaissance-era dish rack made only under the inspiration of your Moses statue." What kind of expression should Michael Angelo have on his face in this situation?

It is foolish for a person to seek inspiration from the works of his contemporaries. Every time I find myself being imitated, I almost feel a physical discomfort.

Decorative art has nothing in common with easel painting. The former is a utilitarian thing, and the latter is a noble pastime. The meaning of a chair is that a person can lean their back on it. This is a product, not art.

In 1906, Cezanne's influence penetrated everywhere. The art of composition, the art of symmetry, and the art of color were very popular for a while. During this period, two questions arose. I saw that painting had an inherent value independent of the faithful reproduction of things. I asked myself, should a person express what he knows or what he sees? Since painting has its own independent beauty, then a person has the possibility of creating an abstract beauty, as long as this beauty does not lose its painterly quality. For many years, the Cubists had no other purpose than the purpose of painting, painting for the sake of painting. They rejected those things that were not the main elements of painting art.

The mathematician Princet often discussed aesthetic problems with us. He had an ideal, wanting to create a geometry specifically for painters to use. This ideal is not new, because some official academies originally used Leonarpo da Vinci's geometry.

The use of color is not extensive, it only represents the elements of the structure in the volume. Everyone knows that a white surface is larger than a black surface of the same size. This theory is not only superficial, but also somewhat naive, but ordinary people spare no effort to insert many painting principles and laws into that superficial theory, and come to me to talk about their painting art.

In my eyes, a painting is by no means a goal, but an occasional pleasure, or an experience. In the field of modeling, color is the standard of measurement. We do not want to confine ourselves to scientific geometry, but there are many people in the world who spend their entire lives searching in this direction with no results, and art is deteriorating.

Cubist painters themselves cannot understand their own works, so they try to invent all kinds of mysterious theories to defend their own works. But Cubism is indeed a free art garden, without any arbitrary dogma. Paintings that are the same Cubist can express the concept of things, or they can express the appearance of things. They can coexist independently without hindering each other.

In fact, people never copy nature, nor do they imitate nature. People only add the clothes of practical form to imagined things. We never abandon painting in order to restore nature. On the contrary, we want to move from nature to painting. Many painters have turned the sun into a yellow dot, but at the same time, some painters, with the help of their art and ingenuity, have turned a yellow dot into a sun. Several elements drawn from nature can make a painting change. Only in this way can we approach the ideals of the great masters of the past who reproduced the natural appearance of things under the guidance of their own concepts.

I firmly believe that in the root of all painting, we can find a subjectively organized illusion, or a spiritual perception like that of Rimband (a modern French painter).

I do not consider the subject matter to be important, but I fully support the object. You must respect the object.

Do not confuse or reverse the key points or order of your most familiar thoughts.

We know that modern art is not the truth.

Art is a lie, this lie guides us closer to the truth, at least it can make us closer to the truths we can think of. A painter should think of ways to enlighten the masses, so that he sees that his lie is the truth.

I think the word "exploration" is really difficult to understand. I believe this word has no meaning. People will never learn from a person who bows his head when walking, hoping that the god of fate will drop a bag of money in front of him. A person who has no intention of exploring but discovers something occasionally will not be admired by the masses, but will be enough to attract their attention.

What I paint is not what I explore, but what I accidentally discover. Intention has no impact on the result. There is a Spanish saying that a person must prove the truth of his love with actions, not with words. The idea of exploring has led many of our painters into a state of emptiness, which can be said to be the biggest mistake of modern art. The spirit of exploring has poisoned many people. Because they do not have the positive aspects of modern art, they want to paint what the naked eye cannot see. What the naked eye cannot see cannot be expressed by art.

What a painting expresses after it is completed is often more than what the painter wants to express. The author is stunned and speculates about the results that were not expected at first.

We can often see that the creation of a painting is natural and unplanned.

People talk about naturalism to resist modern art, but who has ever seen a "natural" work?

Nature and art are two absolutely different phenomena.

Art gives us the possibility to express our concepts and wisdom, but nature has not given us this possibility. From the primitives - their art is far from nature - all the way down to David, Ingres, and Bouguerean, all the painters who reproduced nature deeply knew that art is always art and not nature. From the point of view of art, there is no such thing as an abstract image or a real image. What exists is only the patriarchal expression of the image.

Cubism, like all other schools of painting, is the same in quality and the same principles govern all different schools of painting. Cubism has never been understood, this fact has no important meaning in it, and it does not prove that the opinion of the masses is correct. I do not know German, and a German book is just black and white in my eyes, but I do not arbitrarily say that German does not exist.

Cubism is not a seed of new art, nor is it a sprout of new art, it only represents a period of development of existing painting forms. After these forms are realized, they have the right to exist independently.

If it is said that the current Cubism is still in its infancy, then a new form of Cubism will be produced in the future. Mathematics, geometry, psychopathology and other sciences have been used by people to explain Cubism, those explanations are just literature. Cubism pursues the purpose of modeling, and these purposes themselves can be satisfying. We can explain these purposes as a way to express everything that our intellect and eyes can see within the possible range allowed by images and colors. What an inexhaustible source of pleasure and discovery this is.

Henri Rousseau (Rousseau is a great modern French painter, his paintings are rich in originality) is not strange, but his mental power has developed to a complete degree. The first time I bought one of his oil paintings can be considered a chance encounter. One day I was wandering on Martyr Street and saw a toymaker arranging oil paintings on the wall outside his shop. A portrait caught my attention, the portrait was of a woman's face, with a cold and determined look, completely the look of a French woman. The oil painting was huge. I asked the price, and the merchant said, "Five francs, if you scrape off the things on the canvas, you can repaint a picture on it."

That painting is the most real psychological portrait in the French school.

People often use the term "evolution" and misuse it, which surprises me.

Art has no past and no future. Art that cannot occupy a place in the present will have no place in the future. The art of Greece and the art of Egypt do not belong to the past. They have more vitality today than they had yesterday. Change is not evolution. An artist who changes his expressive power has not changed his heart. Everyone has the right to change, and even painters have this power.

I will always create according to my own policy. I am impatient with the spirit of exploration. I express what I see with my own eyes.

I do not engage in contemplation, nor do I waste time on trying.

When I have something to express, I express it in the way and attitude that I think is most natural.

There is no such thing as transitional art in the world. There are only good and bad painters in the world. Inquisitive journalists and art lovers come to us and force us to tell them our artistic creeds and definitions. You are painters, do they want us to create definitions and maxims?

Yes, the collections of thoughts of Ingres (the giant of the French classical school) and Delaoroix (the master of the French romantic school) have been printed and published, but please ask which of Delaoroix's thoughts can be compared with his painting "Sardananapalusg"?

What is art? If I knew what art was, I would have to keep it a secret.

I don't explore, I just discover occasionally.
